2. **Consolidation** (40% probability): Causal features merged into LucaNet, brand sunset
3. **Spin-out / resale** (20% probability): LucaNet divests Causal if integration fails

**Risk Factors**:
- Acquisition = high uncertainty (pricing, roadmap, support)
- LucaNet is European-focused (US market fit uncertain)
- Pre-acquisition pricing ($250/mo) unsustainable (PE-backed = price increase likely)
- Customer churn risk (acquisition = customer uncertainty)

**Verdict**: High-risk vendor (post-acquisition uncertainty, pricing and roadmap unknown)

## 5-Year Acquisition Predictions (2025-2030)

### High Probability Acquisitions (60-70%)

#### 1. Vena → Microsoft (70% probability by 2028)

**Rationale**:
- **Excel-native synergy**: Vena works inside Excel (Microsoft ecosystem)
- **Dynamics 365 integration**: Vena strong Microsoft Dynamics partnership
- **Microsoft FP&A gap**: Microsoft has no native FP&A platform (only Power BI)
- **PE exit timing**: Hg Capital 5-6 years into hold (typical exit window 5-7 years)

**Acquisition Timeline**: 2026-2028
**Acquisition Price**: $800M-1.5B (8-15x ARR, typical Microsoft CPM acquisition multiple)

**Impact on Customers**:
- **Positive**: Deeper Microsoft 365 integration, Copilot AI features
- **Negative**: Dynamics 365 lock-in pressure, non-Dynamics customers deprioritized

---

#### 2. Prophix → Sage (60% probability by 2027)

**Rationale**:
- **Sage Intacct synergy**: Prophix integrates with Sage Intacct (mid-market ERP)
- **Mid-market focus**: Both target 100-2,000 employee companies
- **PE exit overdue**: Hg Capital 7-8 years into hold (exit imminent)
- **Sage M&A strategy**: Active acquirer (15+ acquisitions in 10 years)

**Acquisition Timeline**: 2025-2027
**Acquisition Price**: $500M-900M (5-9x ARR)

**Impact on Customers**:
- **Positive**: Bundled Sage Intacct + Prophix pricing, deeper ERP integration
- **Negative**: Non-Sage customers deprioritized, feature velocity may slow

---

### Moderate Probability Acquisitions (40-50%)

#### 3. Cube → Microsoft or Snowflake (45% probability by 2029)

**Rationale**:
- **Microsoft scenario** (30% probability): Excel/Google Sheets native synergy, Power BI integration, Dynamics 365 bundle
- **Snowflake scenario** (25% probability): Data warehouse native (Cube queries Snowflake directly), expand data cloud ecosystem
- **Oracle scenario** (20% probability): NetSuite integration strength (Cube strong NetSuite connector)
- **PE exit timing**: Series C March 2024, typical 3-5 year exit window = 2027-2029

**Acquisition Timeline**: 2027-2029 (Series D or strategic acquisition)
**Acquisition Price**: $400M-800M (15-20x ARR if $50M-60M ARR by 2027)

**Impact on Customers**:
- **Microsoft scenario**: Deeper Microsoft 365 integration (Excel Copilot for FP&A), Dynamics 365 bundle, non-Microsoft customers may be deprioritized
- **Snowflake scenario**: Native Snowflake Data Cloud integration, expand to embedded FP&A in warehouse, non-Snowflake customers neutral
- **Oracle scenario**: NetSuite customers benefit (bundle pricing), non-NetSuite customers deprioritized

**Alternative Scenario**: Cube IPO (30% probability) if ARR `>$100M` by 2028, goes public 2029-2030

---

#### 4. Runway → Rippling (40% probability by 2028)

**Rationale**:
- **Rippling partnership**: Runway's #1 integration, 30-40% customers use Rippling
- **SMB suite**: Rippling building full SMB back-office suite (HRIS + payroll + IT + FP&A)
- **Competitive threat**: Gusto, ADP expanding into FP&A (Rippling needs FP&A to compete)
- **Strategic fit**: Runway headcount planning ↔ Rippling HRIS data (seamless)

**Acquisition Timeline**: 2026-2028
**Acquisition Price**: $300M-600M (10-15x ARR, strategic premium)

**Impact on Customers**:
- **Positive**: Bundled Rippling + Runway pricing, native integration depth
- **Negative**: Non-Rippling customers deprioritized, Rippling ecosystem lock-in

**Alternative Acquirer**: Gusto (30% probability), Intuit (15% probability)

---

#### 5. Planful → Oracle or SAP (40% probability by 2030)

**Rationale**:
- **NetSuite synergy**: Planful has 600+ NetSuite customers (Oracle acquisition)
- **PE exit**: Vector Capital / TPG exit in 5-7 years (2025-2027)
- **Enterprise expansion**: Oracle/SAP need mid-market FP&A (OneStream too expensive)

**Acquisition Timeline**: 2027-2030
**Acquisition Price**: $1.5B-3B (8-12x ARR, assuming $250M-300M ARR by 2027)

**Impact on Customers**:
- **Oracle scenario**: NetSuite customers benefit, non-NetSuite deprioritized
- **SAP scenario**: SAP S/4HANA customers benefit, non-SAP deprioritized

**Alternative Scenario**: Planful IPO (50% probability) instead of strategic acquisition

---

### Low Probability Acquisitions (10-20%)

#### 6. Adaptive Insights (Workday) → Standalone IPO (10% probability by 2030)

**Rationale**: Workday spins out Adaptive as standalone public company (rare)
- **Precedent**: PayPal spun out of eBay (2015), VMware spun out of Dell (2021)
- **Rationale**: Adaptive `<10`% of Workday revenue, could unlock value as standalone

**Timeline**: 2028-2030 (unlikely, but possible)

**Impact on Customers**:
- **Positive**: Standalone Adaptive focuses on non-Workday customers (broader market)
- **Negative**: Lose Workday integration depth (no longer same company)

**Verdict**: Very unlikely (Workday has no spin-out history, Adaptive strategically valuable)

---

#### 7. Causal (LucaNet) → Resold or Sunset (20% probability by 2027)

**Rationale**: LucaNet fails to integrate Causal successfully
- **Scenario A**: LucaNet resells Causal to another buyer (Vista Equity, Thoma Bravo)
- **Scenario B**: LucaNet sunsets Causal brand, migrates customers to LucaNet

**Timeline**: 2026-2027 (if integration fails)

**Impact on Customers**:
- **Resale**: Major uncertainty (new owner, new strategy)
- **Sunset**: Forced migration to LucaNet (not US-optimized, European focus)

**Verdict**: Uncertain (wait 12-24 months to see LucaNet integration success/failure)

## 10-Year Survival Probability

| Platform | 5-Year Survival | 10-Year Survival | Notes |
|----------|-----------------|------------------|-------|
| **OneStream** | 99% | 90% | Public company, strong financials |
| **Adaptive (Workday)** | 99.5% | 95% | Large public company, enterprise leader |
| **Anaplan** | 95% | 75% | PE-backed, likely re-IPO 2027-2030 |
| **Planful** | 90% | 70% | PE-backed, likely IPO or strategic sale 2028-2032 |
| **Vena** | 85% | 60% | PE-backed, likely Microsoft acquisition 2026-2028 |
| **Prophix** | 85% | 55% | PE-backed, likely Sage acquisition 2025-2027 |
| **Cube** | 80% | 60% | VC-backed Series C, strong growth, likely acquisition 2027-2030 |
| **Runway** | 75% | 50% | VC-backed, Series D or acquisition 2027-2029 |
| **Causal** | 70% | 50% | Acquired by LucaNet, integration risk |

**Key Insights**:
- **Highest viability**: OneStream, Adaptive (public companies)
- **Moderate viability**: Anaplan, Planful (large PE-backed, exit in 5-7 years)
- **Lower viability**: Vena, Prophix (PE exit imminent, acquisition likely), Cube (VC-backed Series C, acquisition pressure 2027-2030)
- **Highest risk**: Runway (VC-backed, exit pressure), Causal (post-acquisition uncertainty)

---

## Roadmap Stability Assessment

### Public Companies: Predictable (Low Volatility)

**OneStream, Adaptive (Workday)**:
- **Release cadence**: 2-3 major releases/year (quarterly earnings pressure)
- **Feature velocity**: Moderate (incremental improvements, not radical pivots)
- **Predictability**: High (public roadmaps, customer advisory boards)
- **Risk**: Low (established platforms, large customer bases = conservative changes)

**Example**: Adaptive adds AI features over 3 years (2023-2025), not overnight
- 2023: Predictive AI beta
- 2024: General availability
- 2025: Enhanced AI features

**Verdict**: Choose public companies for predictable, stable roadmaps

---

### PE-Backed: Aggressive Growth (Moderate Volatility)

**Anaplan, Planful, Vena, Prophix**:
- **Release cadence**: 3-4 major releases/year (PE pressure to grow)
- **Feature velocity**: High (aggressive feature launches, rapid iteration)
- **Predictability**: Moderate (PE exit pressure = feature bloat risk)
- **Risk**: Moderate (PE exit may change strategy post-sale)

**Example**: Planful launches 4 major features in 2025 (Consolidations Premium, Workforce Pro, AI Assistant, Enhanced Integrations)
- **Positive**: Fast innovation (competitive advantage)
- **Negative**: Feature bloat (complexity increases, user experience suffers)

**Verdict**: PE-backed platforms innovate fast but may over-extend

---

### VC-Backed Startups: High Agility (High Volatility)

**Runway, Causal (pre-acquisition)**:
- **Release cadence**: 4-6 major releases/year (startup speed)
- **Feature velocity**: Very high (rapid iteration, customer feedback loops)
- **Predictability**: Low (pivot risk, competitive pressure)
- **Risk**: High (VC pressure = rapid changes, some features abandoned)

**Example**: Runway launched AI Copilot (July 2024), Ambient Intelligence (same year)
- **Positive**: Fast AI innovation (beat competitors by 12-18 months)
- **Negative**: Beta features (not production-proven, may change significantly)

**Verdict**: VC-backed platforms innovate fastest but highest roadmap volatility

---

## Customer Base Momentum

### Growing (Positive Momentum)

**Runway**: 50+ customers → 200+ customers (2024-2025, 4x growth)
- **Indicator**: Series C funding ($74M), rapid customer acquisition
- **Momentum**: Very Positive (fastest-growing platform in SMB segment)

**Planful**: 1,500 → 2,000+ customers (2023-2025, 33% growth)
- **Indicator**: PE investment, NetSuite partnership expansion
- **Momentum**: Positive (strong mid-market growth)

**OneStream**: 1,400 → 1,600+ customers (2024-2025, 14% growth)
- **Indicator**: IPO, enterprise consolidation wins
- **Momentum**: Positive (steady enterprise growth)

---

### Stable (Neutral Momentum)

**Adaptive**: 3,800 customers (stable, 2023-2025)
- **Indicator**: Mature platform, customer churn = new customer acquisition
- **Momentum**: Neutral (large installed base, slower net-new growth)

**Anaplan**: 2,200 customers (stable, 2023-2025)
- **Indicator**: Mature platform, Thoma Bravo focus on efficiency vs growth
- **Momentum**: Neutral (focus on upselling existing customers vs net-new)

**Prophix**: 2,000+ customers (stable, 2023-2025)
- **Indicator**: Mature mid-market platform, competitive pressure
- **Momentum**: Neutral (replacement cycles, steady state)

---

### Declining (Negative Momentum)

**Vena**: Customer count unknown, but market signals suggest flat-to-declining
- **Indicator**: Excel-native model losing favor to web-native platforms
- **Momentum**: Neutral-to-Negative (Excel dependency = headwind)

**Causal**: Pre-acquisition momentum positive (80-100% growth), post-acquisition uncertain
- **Indicator**: LucaNet acquisition = customer uncertainty
- **Momentum**: Unknown (wait 12-24 months post-acquisition)

---

## 5-Year AI Evolution Outlook (2025-2030)

### Current State (2025): AI Experimentation Phase

**AI Features Available Today**:
- **Tier 1 (Production)**: Runway Ambient Intelligence, Adaptive Predictive AI, Anaplan PlanIQ
- **Tier 2 (Beta)**: Planful Plan Assistant, OneStream AI Agents, Prophix AI, Causal AI
- **Tier 3 (None)**: Vena (no documented AI features)

**AI Pricing**: 10-30% premium (Runway Copilot, Planful AI Assistant)

**AI Maturity**: Early (most features `<2` years old, limited customer feedback)

---

### 2025-2026: AI Becomes Table Stakes

#### What Will Happen

**All Platforms Add AI Features**:
- **Vena**: Announces AI features (2026 roadmap, likely leverage Microsoft Copilot)
- **Causal**: LucaNet integrates AI into consolidated platform
- **Adaptive**: Enhances Workday ML integration (deeper AI across Workday ecosystem)

**AI Pricing Shifts**:
- **2025**: +20-30% subscription premium for AI (early adopter tax)
- **2026**: +10-15% premium (competitive pressure drives down pricing)
- **2027**: Included in base subscription (commoditized)

**AI Accuracy Benchmarks Emerge**:
- Industry standards for AI forecast accuracy (MAPE, RMSE)
- False positive rates for anomaly detection
- User satisfaction scores for variance explanations

**Beta → Production Maturity**:
- Planful Plan Assistant moves to GA (general availability)
- OneStream AI Agents move to GA
- 12-24 months customer feedback validates AI ROI

---

#### What Will Commoditize by 2026-2027

**Natural Language Queries** (90% commoditized by 2027):
- **Today**: Only Runway, Planful, OneStream offer (premium feature)
- **2027**: All platforms offer (table stakes)
- **Example**: "Show me Q3 budget variance by department" (every platform can do this)

**Variance Explanations** (80% commoditized by 2027):
- **Today**: Runway Ambient Intelligence (unique)
- **2027**: All platforms auto-generate variance explanations
- **Differentiation**: Accuracy and relevance (generic vs company-specific)

**Narrative Generation** (70% commoditized by 2027):
- **Today**: Runway, Planful offer (beta/production)
- **2027**: All platforms auto-write board deck commentary
- **Differentiation**: Writing quality (generic boilerplate vs insightful)

---

#### What Remains Differentiated (2026-2027)

**Predictive Forecasting (ML-based)** (50% adoption by 2027):
- **Leaders**: Adaptive (Workday ML), Anaplan (PlanIQ)
- **Laggards**: Runway, Planful (LLM-based, less mature than ML)
- **Differentiation**: Forecast accuracy (Adaptive/Anaplan 7+ years production, others `<2` years)

**Custom LLM Fine-Tuning** (20% adoption by 2027):
- **Early adopters**: Anaplan, Planful offer company-specific AI training
- **Use case**: Train AI on 10 years of company financial narratives (institutional knowledge)
- **Differentiation**: Accuracy on company-specific terminology

**Proactive AI Recommendations** (10% adoption by 2027):
- **Example**: AI recommends "Reduce marketing spend by $50K to hit cash runway target"
- **Leaders**: Runway experiments (2026-2027), others follow
- **Differentiation**: Action-oriented AI (not just insights, but recommendations)

---

### 2027-2028: AI Maturity & Consolidation

#### What Will Happen

**AI Commoditization Accelerates**:
- Natural language queries, variance explanations, narrative generation included in all platforms (no premium)
- Differentiation shifts to accuracy, not availability

**Custom LLMs Become Standard**:
- **All platforms offer**: Fine-tune GPT on company financial policies, terminology, historical narratives
- **Pricing**: +10-20% premium (vs included generic AI)
- **Use case**: Company has 10+ years of board deck commentary → train AI to write in company style

**Proactive AI Emerges**:
- **AI recommends actions**: "Reduce opex by $X to hit EBITDA target" (not just "opex is over budget")
- **Leaders**: Runway, Planful launch proactive AI (2027)
- **Laggards**: Others follow (2028)

**Voice Interfaces Launch**:
- **Example**: "Alexa, what's our Q3 budget variance?" (voice query → FP&A platform → spoken response)
- **Early adopters**: Runway, OneStream (consumer-grade UX focus)
- **Enterprise adoption**: Slow (2028-2030, security concerns)

---

#### What Will Commoditize by 2027-2028

**Predictive Forecasting (ML-based)** (80% commoditized by 2028):
- **Today**: Only Adaptive, Anaplan offer production ML forecasting
- **2027**: Half of platforms offer (mid-market+)
- **2028**: All platforms offer (entry-level may lack)
- **Differentiation**: Forecast accuracy (Adaptive/Anaplan still lead, but gap narrows)

**Custom LLMs (Company-Specific Training)** (50% commoditized by 2028):
- **2025**: Only Runway, Planful offer (premium feature)
- **2028**: All platforms offer custom LLM fine-tuning
- **Differentiation**: Training data quality (garbage in, garbage out)

---

#### What Remains Differentiated (2027-2028)

**Proactive AI Recommendations** (30% adoption by 2028):
- **Leaders**: Runway, Planful (first movers 2027)
- **Laggards**: Adaptive, Anaplan (conservative, wait for customer validation)
- **Differentiation**: Recommendation quality (accurate vs misleading)

**AI Agents (Multi-Step Workflows)** (20% adoption by 2028):
- **Example**: AI Agent completes full budget variance analysis (query data, identify drivers, write narrative, email CFO)
- **Leaders**: OneStream (4 specialized agents), Runway (Copilot evolution)
- **Differentiation**: Agent autonomy (how many steps AI can complete without human)

**Industry-Specific AI** (10% adoption by 2028):
- **Example**: Healthcare forecasting AI (patient volume → revenue), Retail demand forecasting (seasonality, promotions)
- **Leaders**: Anaplan (connected planning, industry-specific models)
- **Differentiation**: Vertical expertise (generic vs healthcare-specific)

---

### 2029-2030: AI-Native FP&A

#### What Will Happen

**AI Replaces Manual Forecasting** (80% automated by 2030):
- **Today**: Analysts build forecasts manually (20-40 hours/month)
- **2030**: AI generates forecasts automatically, analysts review/adjust (2-4 hours/month)
- **Impact**: 80-90% time savings on forecasting

**Real-Time Scenario Planning** (50% adoption by 2030):
- **Today**: Analysts build 3-5 scenarios manually (10-20 hours each)
- **2030**: AI generates 100+ scenarios in seconds, recommends optimal path
- **Example**: "Run 100 scenarios varying churn rate (5-15%) × new sales (80-120% of plan) × opex cuts (0-20%)"

**Embedded AI Everywhere** (90% penetration by 2030):
- **Today**: AI is separate feature (chat interface, opt-in)
- **2030**: Every report, dashboard, chart has AI-generated insights (no manual commentary)
- **Example**: Open budget vs actuals report → AI automatically explains top 5 variances (no query needed)

**AI Market Makers** (New AI-Native Startups Challenge Incumbents):
- **2028-2030**: New AI-native FP&A startups launch (no legacy code debt)
- **Architecture**: Built AI-first (vs retrofitting AI onto 10-year-old platforms)
- **Competitive threat**: Runway-style disruption (modern UX + AI-native architecture)

---

#### What Will Commoditize by 2029-2030

**Proactive AI Recommendations** (80% commoditized by 2030):
- **2027**: Only Runway, Planful offer (premium)
- **2030**: All platforms offer proactive AI recommendations
- **Differentiation**: Recommendation accuracy (AI must earn user trust)

**AI Agents (Multi-Step Workflows)** (60% commoditized by 2030):
- **2025**: Only OneStream offers specialized AI agents
- **2030**: All platforms offer AI agents (varying sophistication)
- **Differentiation**: Agent autonomy + accuracy

**Voice Interfaces** (50% adoption by 2030):
- **2027**: Only Runway, OneStream experiment
- **2030**: Half of platforms offer voice query interfaces
- **Enterprise adoption**: Still slow (security, privacy concerns)

---

#### What Remains Differentiated (2029-2030)

**Company-Specific ML Models** (Never Commoditized):
- **Example**: Fortune 500 retailer trains demand forecasting ML model on 10 years of SKU-level sales data
- **Why not commoditized**: Requires proprietary data + domain expertise (years of development)
- **Platforms can't replicate**: Generic platform AI can't match company-specific proprietary models

**Industry-Specific AI** (30% adoption by 2030, Never Fully Commoditized):
- **Example**: Healthcare revenue cycle forecasting (patient volume, payer mix, regulatory changes)
- **Why not commoditized**: Requires vertical expertise (healthcare CFOs, not generic finance)
- **Leaders**: Anaplan (connected planning, industry models), Adaptive (Workday vertical expertise)

**Proprietary Algorithms** (Never Commoditized):
- **Example**: Anaplan Hyperblock (patented calculation engine), Workday ML (trained on Workday customer data)
- **Why not commoditized**: Years of R&D, proprietary IP
- **Competitive moat**: Technical depth (not replicable by generic LLM)

---

### Custom LLM Opportunities vs Platform AI

#### When to Buy Platform for AI (2025-2027)

**Criteria** (must meet 3+):
1. **No data science team**: `<3` FTEs (can't build custom AI)
2. **Generic use cases**: Budgeting, variance explanations, narrative generation (platform AI handles)
3. **Fast time-to-value**: Need AI in 3-6 months (not 12-24 months custom build)
4. **Limited historical data**: `<5` years financial data (not enough for custom training)

**Recommendation**: Buy Runway, Planful, or Adaptive (production AI features today)

**Timeline**: 2025-2027 (platform AI sufficient for most companies)

---

#### When to Build Custom LLM (2027-2030)

**Criteria** (must meet 4+):
1. **Data science team**: 3+ FTEs already employed (marginal cost low)
2. **Proprietary data**: 10+ years company-specific financial narratives (institutional knowledge)
3. **Unique terminology**: Industry-specific or internal jargon (generic AI fails)
4. **Accuracy critical**: Generic AI explanations insufficient (need company-specific)
5. **Competitive advantage**: Custom AI = proprietary insights (not replicable by competitors)

**Recommendation**: Build custom LLM fine-tuned on company financial policies + historical narratives

**Timeline**: 2027-2030 (after platform AI commoditizes, custom AI = differentiation)

---

#### Hybrid: Platform AI + Custom Fine-Tuning (2028-2030)

**Optimal for most enterprises**:
- **Platform AI** (included): Natural language queries, variance explanations (80% of use cases)
- **Custom fine-tuning** (+10-20% premium): Company-specific terminology, historical narrative style

**Example**: Enterprise uses Planful Plan Assistant (generic AI) + custom LLM trained on 10 years board deck commentary
- **Cost**: $200K Planful + $50K custom fine-tuning = $250K/year
- **Benefit**: Generic AI for 80% of use cases, custom AI for 20% (board decks, investor reports)

**Timeline**: 2028-2030 (after custom LLM infrastructure commoditizes)

---

### When AI Features Will Be Table Stakes vs Premium

| AI Feature | 2025 Status | Table Stakes by | Premium Until |
|------------|-------------|-----------------|---------------|
| **Natural Language Queries** | Premium (+20-30%) | 2027 | 2026 |
| **Variance Explanations** | Premium (+20-30%) | 2027 | 2026 |
| **Narrative Generation** | Premium (+20-30%) | 2027 | 2026 |
| **Predictive Forecasting (ML)** | Premium (+10-20%) | 2028 | 2027 |
| **Custom LLM Fine-Tuning** | Premium (+10-20%) | 2029 | 2028 |
| **Proactive AI Recommendations** | Premium (+20-30%) | 2030 | 2029 |
| **AI Agents (Multi-Step)** | Premium (+30-50%) | Never (?) | 2030+ |
| **Industry-Specific AI** | Premium (+20-40%) | Never | Never |
| **Proprietary Algorithms** | Included | N/A | Never (Competitive Moat) |

**Key Insight**: All AI features commoditize eventually, except proprietary algorithms and industry-specific AI

---

## Vendor Risk Mitigation Strategies

### Strategy 1: Choose Public Companies (Lowest Risk)

**Recommendation**: OneStream, Adaptive (Workday)
- **5-year survival**: 99%+
- **10-year survival**: 90-95%
- **Roadmap stability**: High (predictable, conservative)

**Trade-off**: Lower innovation velocity (vs startups)

---

### Strategy 2: Diversify Vendor Risk (Platform + Data Warehouse)

**Recommendation**: Use FP&A platform for planning + data warehouse for analytics
- **Architecture**: Planful for budgeting → sync data to Snowflake → custom Looker dashboards
- **Benefit**: If Planful acquired/sunset, budgeting data preserved in Snowflake (easier migration)

**Trade-off**: Higher complexity + cost (platform + warehouse)

---

### Strategy 3: Contract Protections (M&A Clauses)

**Recommendation**: Negotiate M&A protection clauses in contract
- **Clause 1**: "If vendor acquired, customer can terminate without penalty"
- **Clause 2**: "If pricing increases `>20`% post-acquisition, customer can exit"
- **Clause 3**: "If product roadmap changes significantly post-acquisition, customer can exit"

**Applicability**: Enterprise contracts only (mid-market+ have leverage)

---

### Strategy 4: Avoid PE Exit Windows (Timing Risk)

**Recommendation**: Avoid vendors in PE exit windows (5-7 years post-acquisition)
- **High risk**: Prophix (7-8 years, exit imminent), Vena (5-6 years, exit 2026-2028)
- **Lower risk**: Anaplan (2 years post-acquisition, exit 2027-2030)

**Strategy**: Choose vendors early in PE cycle (2-4 years post-acquisition) or post-IPO

---

### Strategy 5: Monitor Customer Momentum (Early Warning)

**Recommendation**: Track customer count growth (declining = warning sign)
- **Positive momentum**: Runway (4x growth 2024-2025), Planful (33% growth)
- **Neutral momentum**: Adaptive, Anaplan (stable, mature)
- **Negative momentum**: Vena (Excel-native losing favor), Causal (post-acquisition uncertain)

**Action**: If customer momentum declines 2+ consecutive quarters, evaluate alternatives

---
